          <div data-view-component="true">      A tag already exists with the provided branch name. Many Git commands accept both tag and branch names, so creating this branch may cause unexpected behavior. Are you sure you want to create this branch?
</div>

    </div>
      <footer class="Overlay-footer Overlay-footer--alignEnd">

      </footer>
</modal-dialog></div>

          <a role="menuitem" class="filter-item SelectMenu-item ws-normal wb-break-word line-clamp-2 py-1 " style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; padding-left: 24px;" data-action="click:readme-toc#blur" data-targets="readme-toc.entries" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;repository_toc_menu.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;target&quot;:&quot;entry&quot;,&quot;repository_id&quot;:19872456,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/start/tutorial.md&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:null}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="d73a8b674d841f0294f3326757a034b6c8eb36809e85e46ae7a22d3f4ac2b5b3" href="#jsx-routes">JSX Routes</a>
      </div>
    </div>
  </details-menu>
</details>


  <div class="text-mono f6 flex-auto pr-3 flex-order-2 flex-md-order-1">

      1987 lines (1554 sloc)

<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-tutorial" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tutorial"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Tutorial</h1>
<p dir="auto">Welcome to the tutorial! We'll be building a small, but feature-rich app that lets you keep track of your contacts. We expect it to take between 30-60m if you're following along.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/15.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/15.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Every time you see this it means you need to do something in the app!</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The rest is just there for your information and deeper understanding. Let's get to it.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-setup" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#setup"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Setup</h2>
<p dir="auto">If you're not going to follow along in your own app, you can skip this section</p>
<p dir="auto">We'll be using <a href="https://vitejs.dev/guide/" rel="nofollow">Vite</a> for our bundler and dev server for this tutorial. You'll need <a href="https://nodejs.org" rel="nofollow">Node.js</a> installed for the <code>npm</code> command line tool.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉️</g-emoji> <strong>Open up your terminal and bootstrap a new React app with Vite:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm create vite@latest name-of-your-project -- --template react
# follow prompts
cd &lt;your new project directory&gt;
npm install react-router-dom localforage match-sorter sort-by
npm run dev"><pre>npm create vite@latest name-of-your-project -- --template react
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> follow prompts</span>
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>your new project directory<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>
npm install react-router-dom localforage match-sorter sort-by
npm run dev</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You should be able to visit the URL printed in the terminal:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" VITE v3.0.7  ready in 175 ms

  ➜  Local:   http://127.0.0.1:5173/
  ➜  Network: use --host to expose"><pre class="notranslate"><code> VITE v3.0.7  ready in 175 ms

  ➜  Local:   http://127.0.0.1:5173/
  ➜  Network: use --host to expose
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">We've got some pre-written CSS for this tutorial so we can stay focused on React Router. Feel free to judge it harshly or write your own <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="sweat_smile" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f605.png">😅</g-emoji> (We did things we normally wouldn't in CSS so that the markup in this tutorial could stay as minimal as possible.)</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Copy/Paste the tutorial CSS <a href="https://gist.githubusercontent.com/ryanflorence/ba20d473ef59e1965543fa013ae4163f/raw/499707f25a5690d490c7b3d54c65c65eb895930c/react-router-6.4-tutorial-css.css" rel="nofollow">found here</a> into <code>src/index.css</code></strong></p>
<p dir="auto">This tutorial will be creating, reading, searching, updating, and deleting data. A typical web app would probably be talking to an API on your web server, but we're going to use browser storage and fake some network latency to keep this focused. None of this code is relevant to React Router, so just go ahead and copy/paste it all.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Copy/Paste the tutorial data module <a href="https://gist.githubusercontent.com/ryanflorence/1e7f5d3344c0db4a8394292c157cd305/raw/f7ff21e9ae7ffd55bfaaaf320e09c6a08a8a6611/contacts.js" rel="nofollow">found here</a> into <code>src/contacts.js</code></strong></p>
<p dir="auto">All you need in the src folder are <code>contacts.js</code>, <code>main.jsx</code>, and <code>index.css</code>. You can delete anything else (like <code>App.js</code> and <code>assets</code>, etc.).</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Delete unused files in <code>src/</code> so all you have left are these:</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="src
├── contacts.js
├── index.css
└── main.jsx"><pre class="notranslate"><code>src
├── contacts.js
├── index.css
└── main.jsx
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If your app is running, it might blow up momentarily, just keep going <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="yum" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f60b.png">😋</g-emoji>. And with that, we're ready to get started!</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-adding-a-router" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#adding-a-router"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Adding a Router</h2>
<p dir="auto">First thing to do is create a <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/routers/create-browser-router">Browser Router</a> and configure our first route. This will enable client side routing for our web app.</p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>main.jsx</code> file is the entry point. Open it up and we'll put React Router on the page.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create and render a <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/routers/create-browser-router">browser router</a> in <code>main.jsx</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import React from &quot;react&quot;;
import ReactDOM from &quot;react-dom/client&quot;;
import {
  createBrowserRouter,
  RouterProvider,
  Route,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import &quot;./index.css&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;div&gt;Hello world!&lt;/div&gt;,
  },
]);

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById(&quot;root&quot;)).render(
  &lt;React.StrictMode&gt;
    &lt;RouterProvider router={router} /&gt;
  &lt;/React.StrictMode&gt;
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">React</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ReactDOM</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-dom/client"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">RouterProvider</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Route</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s">"./index.css"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Hello world!<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-v">ReactDOM</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">createRoot</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getElementById</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"root"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">render</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">React</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">StrictMode</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">RouterProvider</span> <span class="pl-c1">router</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">router</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-v">React</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">StrictMode</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This first route is what we often call the "root route" since the rest of our routes will render inside of it. It will serve as the root layout of the UI, we'll have nested layouts as we get farther along.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-the-root-route" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-root-route"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The Root Route</h2>
<p dir="auto">Let's add the global layout for this app.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create <code>src/routes</code> and <code>src/routes/root.jsx</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="mkdir src/routes
touch src/routes/root.jsx"><pre>mkdir src/routes
touch src/routes/root.jsx</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">(If you don't want to be a command line nerd, use your editor instead of those commands <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="nerd_face" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f913.png">🤓</g-emoji>)</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the root layout component</strong></p>

<p dir="auto">Nothing React Router specific yet, so feel free to copy/paste all of that.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Set <code>&lt;Root&gt;</code> as the root route's <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/route#element"><code>element</code></a></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* existing imports */
import Root from &quot;./routes/root&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
  },
]);

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById(&quot;root&quot;)).render(
  &lt;React.StrictMode&gt;
    &lt;RouterProvider router={router} /&gt;
  &lt;/React.StrictMode&gt;

<p dir="auto">The app should look something like this now. It sure is nice having a designer who can also write the CSS, isn't it? <p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/01.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/01.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-handling-not-found-errors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#handling-not-found-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Handling Not Found Errors</h2>
<p dir="auto">It's always a good idea to know how your app responds to errors early in the project because we all write far more bugs than features when building a new app! Not only will your users get a good experience when this happens, but it helps you during development as well.</p>
<p dir="auto">We added some links to this app, let's see what happens when we click them?</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Click one of the sidebar names</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/02.webp"><img alt="screenshot of default React Router error element" src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/02.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Gross! This is the default error screen in React Router, made worse by our flex box styles on the root element in this app <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="joy" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f602.png">😂</g-emoji>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Anytime your app throws an error while rendering, loading data, or performing data mutations, React Router will catch it and render an error screen. Let's make our own error page.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create an error page component</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="touch src/error-page.jsx"><pre>touch src/error-page.jsx</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { useRouteError } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function ErrorPage() {
  const error = useRouteError();
  console.error(error);

  return (
    &lt;div id=&quot;error-page&quot;&gt;
      &lt;h1&gt;Oops!&lt;/h1&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;Sorry, an unexpected error has occurred.&lt;/p&gt;
      &lt;p&gt;
        &lt;i&gt;{error.statusText || error.message}&lt;/i&gt;
      &lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">useRouteError</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">ErrorPage</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useRouteError</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">console</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"error-page"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Oops!<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Sorry, an unexpected error has occurred.<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">statusText</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">error</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">message</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Set the <code>&lt;ErrorPage&gt;</code> as the <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/error-element"><code>errorElement</code></a> on the root route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* previous imports */
import ErrorPage from &quot;./error-page&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
  },
]);

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById(&quot;root&quot;)).render(
  &lt;React.StrictMode&gt;
    &lt;RouterProvider router={router} /&gt;
  &lt;/React.StrictMode&gt;
);"><pre><span class="pl-c">/* previous imports */</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"./error-page"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-v">ReactDOM</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">createRoot</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getElementById</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"root"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">render</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-v">React</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">StrictMode</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">RouterProvider</span> <span class="pl-c1">router</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">router</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-v">React</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">StrictMode</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The error page should now look like this:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/03.webp"><img alt="new error page, but still ugly" src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/03.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">(Well, that's not much better. Maybe somebody forgot to ask the designer to make an error page. Maybe everybody forgets to ask the designer to make an error page and then blames the designer for not thinking of it <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="laughing" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f606.png">😆</g-emoji>)</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-route-error"><code>useRouteError</code></a> provides the error that was thrown. When the user navigates to routes that don't exist you'll get an <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/utils/is-route-error-response">error response</a> with a "Not Found" <code>statusText</code>. We'll see some other errors later in the tutorial and discuss them more.</p>
<p dir="auto">For now, it's enough to know that pretty much all of your errors will now be handled by this page instead of infinite spinners, unresponsive pages, or blank screens <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="raised_hands" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f64c.png">🙌</g-emoji></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-the-contact-route-ui" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#the-contact-route-ui"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>The Contact Route UI</h2>
<p dir="auto">Instead of a 404 "Not Found" page, we want to actually render something at the URLs we've linked to. For that, we need to make a new route.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the contact route module</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="touch src/routes/contact.jsx"><pre>touch src/routes/contact.jsx</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the contact component UI</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">It's just a bunch of elements, feel free to copy/paste.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Form } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function Contact() {
  const contact = {
    first: &quot;Your&quot;,
    last: &quot;Name&quot;,
    avatar: &quot;https://placekitten.com/g/200/200&quot;,
    twitter: &quot;your_handle&quot;,
    notes: &quot;Some notes&quot;,
    favorite: true,
  };

  return (
    &lt;div id=&quot;contact&quot;&gt;
      &lt;div&gt;
        &lt;img
          key={contact.avatar}
          src={contact.avatar || null}
        /&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;

      &lt;div&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;
          {contact.first || contact.last ? (
            &lt;&gt;
              {contact.first} {contact.last}
            &lt;/&gt;
          ) : (
            &lt;i&gt;No Name&lt;/i&gt;
          )}{&quot; &quot;}
          &lt;Favorite contact={contact} /&gt;
        &lt;/h1&gt;

        {contact.twitter &amp;&amp; (
          &lt;p&gt;
            &lt;a
              target=&quot;_blank&quot;
              href={`https://twitter.com/${contact.twitter}`}
            &gt;
              {contact.twitter}
            &lt;/a&gt;
          &lt;/p&gt;
        )}

        {contact.notes &amp;&amp; &lt;p&gt;{contact.notes}&lt;/p&gt;}

        &lt;div&gt;
          &lt;Form action=&quot;edit&quot;&gt;
            &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot;&gt;Edit&lt;/button&gt;
          &lt;/Form&gt;
          &lt;Form
            method=&quot;post&quot;
            action=&quot;destroy&quot;
            onSubmit={(event) =&gt; {
              if (
                !confirm(
                  &quot;Please confirm you want to delete this record.&quot;
                )
              ) {
                event.preventDefault();
              }
            }}
          &gt;
            &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot;&gt;Delete&lt;/button&gt;
          &lt;/Form&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  );
}

function Favorite({ contact }) {
  // yes, this is a `let` for later
  let favorite = contact.favorite;
  return (
    &lt;Form method=&quot;post&quot;&gt;
      &lt;button
        name=&quot;favorite&quot;
        value={favorite ? &quot;false&quot; : &quot;true&quot;}
        aria-label={
          favorite
            ? &quot;Remove from favorites&quot;
            : &quot;Add to favorites&quot;
        }
      &gt;
        {favorite ? &quot;★&quot; : &quot;☆&quot;}
      &lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;/Form&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Form</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Contact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">first</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Your"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">last</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Name"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">avatar</span>: <span class="pl-s">"https://placekitten.com/g/200/200"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">twitter</span>: <span class="pl-s">"your_handle"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">notes</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Some notes"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">favorite</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"contact"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">first</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">last</span> ? <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">first</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">last</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">)</span> : <span class="pl-kos">(</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

              <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">twitter</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"submit"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Edit<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Favorite</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> contact <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">value</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"false"</span> : <span class="pl-s">"true"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"★"</span> : <span class="pl-s">"☆"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Now that we've got a component, let's hook it up to a new route.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Import the contact component and create a new route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* existing imports */
import Contact from &quot;./routes/contact&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
  },
  {
    path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
    element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
  },
]);

/* existing code */"><pre><span class="pl-c">/* existing imports */</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Contact</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"./routes/contact"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Now if we click one of the links or visit <code>/contacts/1</code> we get our new component!</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/04.webp"><img alt="contact route rendering without the parent layout" src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/04.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">However, it's not inside of our root layout <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="angry" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f620.png">😠</g-emoji></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-nested-routes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#nested-routes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Nested Routes</h2>
<p dir="auto">We want the contact component to render <em>inside</em> of the <code>&lt;Root&gt;</code> layout like this.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/05.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/05.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We do it by making the contact route a <em>child</em> of the root route.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Move the contacts route to be a child of the root route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    children: [
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
      },
    ],
  },
]);"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You'll now see the root layout again but a blank page on the right. We need to tell the root route <em>where</em> we want it to render its child routes. We do that with <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/outlet"><code>&lt;Outlet&gt;</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Find the <code>&lt;div id="detail"&gt;</code> and put an outlet inside</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Render an <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/outlet"><code>&lt;Outlet&gt;</code></a></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Outlet } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function Root() {
  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      {/* all the other elements */}
      &lt;div id=&quot;detail&quot;&gt;
        &lt;Outlet /&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* all the other elements */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"detail"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Outlet</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-client-side-routing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#client-side-routing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Client Side Routing</h2>
<p dir="auto">You may or may not have noticed, but when we click the links in the sidebar, the browser is doing a full document request for the next URL instead of using React Router.</p>
<p dir="auto">Client side routing allows our app to update the URL without requesting another document from the server. Instead, the app can immediately render new UI. Let's make it happen with <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/link"><code>&lt;Link&gt;</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Change the sidebar <code>&lt;a href&gt;</code> to <code>&lt;Link to&gt;</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Outlet, Link } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function Root() {
  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        {/* other elements */}

        &lt;nav&gt;
          &lt;ul&gt;
            &lt;li&gt;
              &lt;Link to={`contacts/1`}&gt;Your Name&lt;/Link&gt;
            &lt;/li&gt;
            &lt;li&gt;
              &lt;Link to={`contacts/2`}&gt;Your Friend&lt;/Link&gt;
            &lt;/li&gt;
          &lt;/ul&gt;
        &lt;/nav&gt;

        {/* other elements */}
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">Link</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other elements */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">nav</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Link</span> <span class="pl-c1">to</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">`contacts/1`</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Your Name<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Link</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Link</span> <span class="pl-c1">to</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">`contacts/2`</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Your Friend<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Link</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">nav</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other elements */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can open the network tab in the browser devtools to see that it's not requesting documents anymore.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-loading-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#loading-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Loading Data</h2>
<p dir="auto">URL segments, layouts, and data are more often than not coupled (tripled?) together. We can see it in this app already:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>URL Segment</th>
<th>Component</th>
<th>Data</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>/</td>
<td><code>&lt;Root&gt;</code></td>
<td>list of contacts</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>contacts/:id</td>
<td><code>&lt;Contact&gt;</code></td>
<td>individual contact</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p dir="auto">Because of this natural coupling, React Router has data conventions to get data into your route components easily.</p>
<p dir="auto">There are two APIs we'll be using to load data, <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/loader"><code>loader</code></a> and <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-loader-data"><code>useLoaderData</code></a>. First we'll create and export a loader function in the root module, then we'll hook it up to the route. Finally, we'll access and render the data.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Export a loader from <code>root.jsx</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Outlet, Link } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { getContacts } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function loader() {
  const contacts = await getContacts();
  return { contacts };
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-v">Link</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getContacts</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">loader</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contacts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">getContacts</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Configure the loader on the route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* other imports */
import Root, { loader as rootLoader } from &quot;./routes/root&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    children: [
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
      },
    ],
  },
]);"><pre><span class="pl-c">/* other imports */</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">loader</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"./routes/root"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">loader</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Access and render the data</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  Outlet,
  Link,
  useLoaderData,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { getContacts } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

/* other code */

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts } = useLoaderData();
  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;React Router Contacts&lt;/h1&gt;
        {/* other code */}

        &lt;nav&gt;
          {contacts.length ? (
            &lt;ul&gt;
              {contacts.map((contact) =&gt; (
                &lt;li key={contact.id}&gt;
                  &lt;Link to={`contacts/${contact.id}`}&gt;
                    {contact.first || contact.last ? (
                      &lt;&gt;
                        {contact.first} {contact.last}
                      &lt;/&gt;
                    ) : (
                      &lt;i&gt;No Name&lt;/i&gt;
                    )}{&quot; &quot;}
                    {contact.favorite &amp;&amp; &lt;span&gt;★&lt;/span&gt;}
                  &lt;/Link&gt;
                &lt;/li&gt;
              ))}
            &lt;/ul&gt;
          ) : (
            &lt;p&gt;
              &lt;i&gt;No contacts&lt;/i&gt;
            &lt;/p&gt;
          )}
        &lt;/nav&gt;

        {/* other code */}
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Link</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getContacts</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>React Router Contacts<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">nav</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contacts</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span> ? <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contacts</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
                <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span> <span class="pl-c1">key</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Link</span> <span class="pl-c1">to</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">`contacts/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                    <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">first</span> <span class="pl-c1">||</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">last</span> ? <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
                      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">first</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">last</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
                      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                    <span class="pl-kos">)</span> : <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
                      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>No Name<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                    <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">" "</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
                    <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">favorite</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>★<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">span</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
                  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Link</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">)</span> : <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>No contacts<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">i</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">nav</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">That's it! React Router will now automatically keep that data in sync with your UI. We don't have any data yet, so you're probably getting a blank list like this:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/06.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/06.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-data-writes--html-forms" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#data-writes--html-forms"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Data Writes + HTML Forms</h2>
<p dir="auto">We'll create our first contact in a second, but first let's talk about HTML.</p>
<p dir="auto">React Router emulates HTML Form navigation as the data mutation primitive, according to web development before the JavaScript cambrian explosion. It gives you the UX capabilities of client rendered apps with the simplicity of the "old school" web model.</p>
<p dir="auto">While unfamiliar to some web developers, HTML forms actually cause a navigation in the browser, just like clicking a link. The only difference is in the request: links can only change the URL while forms can also change the request method (GET vs POST) and the request body (POST form data).</p>
<p dir="auto">Without client side routing, the browser will serialize the form's data automatically and send it to the server as the request body for POST, and as URLSearchParams for GET. React Router does the same thing, except instead of sending the request to the server, it uses client side routing and sends it to a route <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/action"><code>action</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">We can test this out by clicking the "New" button in our app. The app should blow up because the Vite server isn't configured to handle a POST request (it sends a 404, though it should probably be a 405 <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="shrug" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f937.png">🤷</g-emoji>).</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/07.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/07.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Instead of sending that POST to the Vite server to create a new contact, let's use client side routing instead.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-creating-contacts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#creating-contacts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Creating Contacts</h2>
<p dir="auto">We'll create new contacts by exporting an <code>action</code> in our root route, wiring it up to the route config, and changing our <code>&lt;form&gt;</code> to a React Router <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/form"><code>&lt;Form&gt;</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the action and change <code>&lt;form&gt;</code> to <code>&lt;Form&gt;</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  Outlet,
  Link,
  useLoaderData,
  Form,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { getContacts, createContact } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function action() {
  await createContact();
}

/* other code */

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts } = useLoaderData();
  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;

        &lt;div&gt;
          {/* other code */}
          &lt;Form method=&quot;post&quot;&gt;
            &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot;&gt;New&lt;/button&gt;
          &lt;/Form&gt;
        &lt;/div&gt;

        {/* other code */}
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );

  <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Link</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getContacts</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">createContact</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">createContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>React Router Contacts<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">method</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"post"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"submit"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>New<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Import and set the action on the route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* other imports */

import Root, {
  loader as rootLoader,
  action as rootAction,
} from &quot;./routes/root&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    action: rootAction,
    children: [
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
      },
    ],
  },
]);"><pre><span class="pl-c">/* other imports */</span>

<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">loader</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">action</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">rootAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"./routes/root"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">loader</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">That's it! Go ahead and click the "New" button and you should see a new record pop into the list <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="partying_face" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f973.png">🥳</g-emoji></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/08.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/08.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>createContact</code> method just creates an empty contact with no name or data or anything. But it does still create a record, promise!</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="monocle_face" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f9d0.png">🧐</g-emoji> Wait a sec ... How did the sidebar update? Where did we call the <code>action</code>? Where's the code to refetch the data? Where are <code>useState</code>, <code>onSubmit</code> and <code>useEffect</code>?!</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">This is where the "old school web" programming model shows up. As we discussed earlier, <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/form"><code>&lt;Form&gt;</code></a> prevents the browser from sending the request to the server and sends it to your route <code>action</code> instead. In web semantics, a POST usually means some data is changing. By convention, React Router uses this as a hint to automatically revalidate the data on the page after the action finishes. That means all of your <code>useLoaderData</code> hooks update and the UI stays in sync with your data automatically! Pretty cool.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-url-params-in-loaders" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#url-params-in-loaders"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>URL Params in Loaders</h2>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Click on the No Name record</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">We should be seeing our old static contact page again, with one difference: the URL now has a real ID for the record.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/09.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/09.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Reviewing the route config, the route looks like this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[
  {
    path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
    element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
  },
];"><pre><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note the <code>:contactId</code> URL segment. The colon (<code>:</code>) has special meaning, turning it into a "dynamic segment". Dynamic segments will match dynamic (changing) values in that position of the URL, like the contact ID. We call these values in the URL "URL Params", or just "params" for short.</p>
<p dir="auto">These <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/loader#params"><code>params</code></a> are passed to the loader with keys that match the dynamic segment. For example, our segment is named <code>:contactId</code> so the value will be passed as <code>params.contactId</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">These params are most often used to find a record by ID. Let's try it out.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add a loader to the contact page and access data with <code>useLoaderData</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Form, useLoaderData } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { getContact } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function loader({ params }) {
  return getContact(params.contactId);
}

export default function Contact() {
  const contact = useLoaderData();
  // existing code
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getContact</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">loader</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Configure the loader on the route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* existing code */

  loader as contactLoader,
} from &quot;./routes/contact&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,

    children: [
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
        loader: contactLoader,
      },
    ],
  },
]);
