<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/10.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/10.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-updating-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#updating-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Updating Data</h2>
<p dir="auto">Just like creating data, you update data with <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/form"><code>&lt;Form&gt;</code></a>. Let's make a new route at <code>contacts/:contactId/edit</code>. Again, we'll start with the component and then wire it up to the route config.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the edit component</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="touch src/routes/edit.jsx"><pre class="notranslate"><code>touch src/routes/edit.jsx
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the edit page UI</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Nothing we haven't seen before, feel free to copy/paste:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { Form, useLoaderData } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the new edit route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* existing code */
import EditContact from &quot;./routes/edit&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    action: rootAction,
    children: [
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
        loader: contactLoader,
      },
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId/edit&quot;,
        element: &lt;EditContact /&gt;,
        loader: contactLoader,
      },
    ],
  },
]);

/* existing code */"><pre><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

<span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">We want it to be rendered in the root route's outlet, so we made it a sibling to the existing child route.</p>
<p dir="auto">(You might note we reused the <code>contactLoader</code> for this route. This is only because we're being lazy in the tutorial. There is no reason to attempt to share loaders among routes, they usually have their own.)</p>
<p dir="auto">Alright, clicking the "Edit" button gives us this new UI:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/11.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/11.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-updating-contacts-with-formdata" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#updating-contacts-with-formdata"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Updating Contacts with FormData</h2>
<p dir="auto">The edit route we just created already renders a form. All we need to do to update the record is wire up an action to the route. The form will post to the action and the data will be automatically revalidated.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add an action to the edit module</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  Form,
  useLoaderData,
  redirect,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { updateContact } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function action({ request, params }) {
  const formData = await request.formData();
  const updates = Object.fromEntries(formData);
  await updateContact(params.contactId, updates);
  return redirect(`/contacts/${params.contactId}`);
}

/* existing code */"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">updateContact</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> request<span class="pl-kos">,</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">formData</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">updates</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">fromEntries</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">updateContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">updates</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">`/contacts/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Wire the action up to the route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* existing code */
import EditContact, {
  action as editAction,
} from &quot;./routes/edit&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    action: rootAction,
    children: [
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
        loader: contactLoader,
      },
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId/edit&quot;,
        element: &lt;EditContact /&gt;,
        loader: contactLoader,
        action: editAction,
      },
    ],
  },
]);

<p dir="auto">Fill out the form, hit save, and you should see something like this! (Except easier on the eyes and maybe less hairy.)</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/12.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/12.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-mutation-discussion" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mutation-discussion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Mutation Discussion</h2>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="expressionless" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f611.png">😑</g-emoji> It worked, but I have no idea what is going on here...</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Let's dig in a bit...</p>
<p dir="auto">Open up <code>src/routes/edit.jsx</code> and look at the form elements. Notice how they each have a name:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;input
  placeholder=&quot;First&quot;
  aria-label=&quot;First name&quot;
  type=&quot;text&quot;
  name=&quot;first&quot;
  defaultValue={contact.first}
/&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">placeholder</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"First"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">aria-label</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"First name"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"text"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"first"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">defaultValue</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">first</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Without JavaScript, when a form is submitted, the browser will create <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/FormData" rel="nofollow"><code>FormData</code></a> and set it as the body of the request when it sends it to the server. As mentioned before, React Router prevents that and sends the request to your action instead, including the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/FormData" rel="nofollow"><code>FormData</code></a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Each field in the form is accessible with <code>formData.get(name)</code>. For example, given the input field from above, you could access the first and last names like this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export async function action({ request, params }) {
  const formData = await request.formData();
  const firstName = formData.get(&quot;first&quot;);
  const lastName = formData.get(&quot;last&quot;);
  // ...
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> request<span class="pl-kos">,</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">formData</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">firstName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"first"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">lastName</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"last"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// ...</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Since we have a handful of form fields, we used <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object/fromEntries" rel="nofollow"><code>Object.fromEntries</code></a> to collect them all into an object, which is exactly what our <code>updateContact</code> function wants.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const updates = Object.fromEntries(formData);
updates.first; // &quot;Some&quot;
updates.last; // &quot;Name&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">updates</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">fromEntries</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-s1">updates</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">first</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// "Some"</span>
<span class="pl-s1">updates</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">last</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-c">// "Name"</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Aside from <code>action</code>, none of these APIs we're discussing are provided by React Router: <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Request" rel="nofollow"><code>request</code></a>, <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Request/formData" rel="nofollow"><code>request.formData</code></a>, <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object/fromEntries" rel="nofollow"><code>Object.fromEntries</code></a> are all provided by the web platform.</p>
<p dir="auto">After we finished the action, note the <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/fetch/redirect"><code>redirect</code></a> at the end:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export async function action({ request, params }) {
  const formData = await request.formData();
  const updates = Object.fromEntries(formData);
  await updateContact(params.contactId, updates);
  return redirect(`/contacts/${params.contactId}`);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> request<span class="pl-kos">,</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">formData</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">updates</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Object</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">fromEntries</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">updateContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">updates</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">`/contacts/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Loaders and actions can both <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/loader#returning-responses">return a <code>Response</code></a> (makes sense, since they received a <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Request" rel="nofollow"><code>Request</code></a>!). The <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/fetch/redirect"><code>redirect</code></a> helper just makes it easier to return a <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Response" rel="nofollow">response</a> that tells the app to change locations.</p>
<p dir="auto">Without client side routing, if a server redirected after a POST request, the new page would fetch the latest data and render. As we learned before, React Router emulates this model and automatically revalidates the data on the page after the action. That's why the sidebar automatically updates when we save the form. The extra revalidation code doesn't exist without client side routing, so it doesn't need to exist with client side routing either!</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-redirecting-new-records-to-the-edit-page" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#redirecting-new-records-to-the-edit-page"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Redirecting new records to the edit page</h2>
<p dir="auto">Now that we know how to redirect, let's update the action that creates new contacts to redirect to the edit page:</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Redirect to the new record's edit page</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  Outlet,
  Link,
  useLoaderData,
  Form,
  redirect,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { getContacts, createContact } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function action() {
  const contact = await createContact();
  return redirect(`/contacts/${contact.id}/edit`);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Link</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getContacts</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">createContact</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">createContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">`/contacts/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/edit`</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Now when we click "New", we should end up on the edit page:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/13.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/13.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add a handful of records</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">I'm going to use the stellar lineup of speakers from the first Remix Conference <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="grin" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f601.png">😁</g-emoji></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/14.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/14.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-active-link-styling" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#active-link-styling"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Active Link Styling</h2>
<p dir="auto">Now that we have a bunch of records, it's not clear which one we're looking at in the sidebar. We can use <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/components/nav-link"><code>NavLink</code></a> to fix this.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Use a <code>NavLink</code> in the sidebar</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  Outlet,
  NavLink,
  useLoaderData,
  Form,
  redirect,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function Root() {
  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        {/* other code */}

        &lt;nav&gt;
          {contacts.length ? (
            &lt;ul&gt;
              {contacts.map((contact) =&gt; (
                &lt;li key={contact.id}&gt;
                  &lt;NavLink
                    to={`contacts/${contact.id}`}
                    className={({ isActive, isPending }) =&gt;
                      isActive
                        ? &quot;active&quot;
                        : isPending
                        ? &quot;pending&quot;
                        : &quot;&quot;
                    }
                  &gt;
                    {/* other code */}
                  &lt;/NavLink&gt;
                &lt;/li&gt;
              ))}
            &lt;/ul&gt;
          ) : (
            &lt;p&gt;{/* other code */}&lt;/p&gt;
          )}
        &lt;/nav&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Outlet</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">NavLink</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">nav</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contacts</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">length</span> ? <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contacts</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">map</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
                <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span> <span class="pl-c1">key</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">NavLink</span>
                    <span class="pl-c1">to</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">`contacts/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">${</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>`</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
                    <span class="pl-c1">className</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> isActive<span class="pl-kos">,</span> isPending <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span>
                      <span class="pl-s1">isActive</span>
                        ? <span class="pl-s">"active"</span>
                        : <span class="pl-s1">isPending</span>
                        ? <span class="pl-s">"pending"</span>
                        : <span class="pl-s">""</span>
                    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
                  <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                    <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
                  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">NavLink</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
                <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">li</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">ul</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">)</span> : <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* other code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">nav</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note that we are passing a function to <code>className</code>. When the user is at the URL in the <code>NavLink</code>, then <code>isActive</code> will be true. When it's <em>about</em> to be active (the data is still loading) then <code>isPending</code> will be true. This allows us to easily indicate where the user is, as well as provide immediate feedback on links that have been clicked but we're still waiting for data to load.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/15.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/15.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-global-pending-ui" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#global-pending-ui"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Global Pending UI</h2>
<p dir="auto">As the user navigates the app, React Router will <em>leave the old page up</em> as data is loading for the next page. You may have noticed the app feels a little unresponsive as you click between the list. Let's provide the user with some feedback so the app doesn't feel unresponsive.</p>
<p dir="auto">React Router is managing all of the state behind the scenes and reveals the pieces of it you need to build dynamic web apps. In this case, we'll use the <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-navigation"><code>useNavigation</code></a> hook.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong><code>useNavigation</code> to add global pending UI</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  // existing code
  useNavigation,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

// existing code

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts } = useLoaderData();
  const navigation = useNavigation();

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;{/* existing code */}&lt;/div&gt;
      &lt;div
        id=&quot;detail&quot;
        className={
          navigation.state === &quot;loading&quot; ? &quot;loading&quot; : &quot;&quot;
        }
      &gt;
        &lt;Outlet /&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useNavigation</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">navigation</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useNavigation</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"detail"</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">className</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">navigation</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">state</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"loading"</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"loading"</span> : <span class="pl-s">""</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Outlet</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-navigation"><code>useNavigation</code></a> returns the current navigation state: it can be one of <code>"idle" | "submitting" | "loading"</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">In our case, we add a <code>"loading"</code> class to the main part of the app if we're not idle. The CSS then adds a nice fade after a short delay (to avoid flickering the UI for fast loads). You could do anything you want though, like show a spinner or loading bar across the top.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/16.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/16.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Note that our data model (<code>src/contact.js</code>) has a clientside cache, so navigating to the same contact is fast the second time. This behavior is <em>not</em> React Router, it will re-load data for changing routes no matter if you've been there before or not. It does, however, avoid calling the loaders for <em>unchanging</em> routes (like the list) during a navigation.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-deleting-records" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#deleting-records"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Deleting Records</h2>
<p dir="auto">If we review code in the contact route, we can find the delete button looks like this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;Form
  method=&quot;post&quot;
  action=&quot;destroy&quot;
  onSubmit={(event) =&gt; {
    if (
      !confirm(
        &quot;Please confirm you want to delete this record.&quot;
      )
    ) {
      event.preventDefault();
    }
  }}
&gt;
  &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot;&gt;Delete&lt;/button&gt;
&lt;/Form&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">method</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"post"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"destroy"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">onSubmit</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">event</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-en">confirm</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
        <span class="pl-s">"Please confirm you want to delete this record."</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">)</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-s1">event</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">preventDefault</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
<span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"submit"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Delete<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note the <code>action</code> points to <code>"destroy"</code>. Like <code>&lt;Link to&gt;</code>, <code>&lt;Form action&gt;</code> can take a <em>relative</em> value. Since the form is rendered in <code>contact/:contactId</code>, then a relative action with <code>destroy</code> will submit the form to <code>contact/:contactId/destroy</code> when clicked.</p>
<p dir="auto">At this point you should know everything you need to know to make the delete button work. Maybe give it a shot before moving on? You'll need:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>A new route</li>
<li>An <code>action</code> at that route</li>
<li><code>deleteContact</code> from <code>src/contacts.js</code></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the "destroy" route module</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="touch src/routes/destroy.jsx"><pre class="notranslate"><code>touch src/routes/destroy.jsx
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the destroy action</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { redirect } from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;
import { deleteContact } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function action({ params }) {
  await deleteContact(params.contactId);
  return redirect(&quot;/&quot;);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">redirect</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">deleteContact</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">deleteContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the destroy route to the route config</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="/* existing code */
import { action as destroyAction } from &quot;./routes/destroy&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    /* existing root route props */
    children: [
      /* existing routes */
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId/destroy&quot;,
        action: destroyAction,
      },
    ],
  },
]);

/* existing code */"><pre><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">action</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">destroyAction</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"./routes/destroy"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c">/* existing root route props */</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-c">/* existing routes */</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId/destroy"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">destroyAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alright, navigate to a record and click the "Delete" button. It works!</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="sweat_smile" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f605.png">😅</g-emoji> I'm still confused why this all works</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">When the user clicks the submit button:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><code>&lt;Form&gt;</code> prevents the default browser behavior of sending a new POST request to the server, but instead emulates the browser by creating a POST request with client side routing</li>
<li>The <code>&lt;Form action="destroy"&gt;</code> matches the new route at <code>"contacts/:contactId/destroy"</code> and sends it the request</li>
<li>After the action redirects, React Router calls all of the loaders for the data on the page to get the latest values (this is "revalidation"). <code>useLoaderData</code> returns new values and causes the components to update!</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Add a form, add an action, React Router does the rest.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-contextual-errors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#contextual-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Contextual Errors</h2>
<p dir="auto">Just for kicks, throw an error in the destroy action:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export async function action({ params }) {
  throw new Error(&quot;oh dang!&quot;);
  await deleteContact(params.contactId);
  return redirect(&quot;/&quot;);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Error</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"oh dang!"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">deleteContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/17.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/17.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Recognize that screen? It's our <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/error-element"><code>errorElement</code></a> from before. The user, however, can't really do anything to recover from this screen except to hit refresh.</p>
<p dir="auto">Let's create a contextual error message for the destroy route:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[
  /* other routes */
  {
    path: &quot;contacts/:contactId/destroy&quot;,
    action: destroyAction,
    errorElement: &lt;div&gt;Oops! There was an error.&lt;/div&gt;,
  },
];"><pre><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-c">/* other routes */</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId/destroy"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">destroyAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Oops! There was an error.<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Now try it again:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/18.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/18.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Our user now has more options than slamming refresh, they can continue to interact with the parts of the page that aren't having trouble <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="raised_hands" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f64c.png">🙌</g-emoji></p>
<p dir="auto">Because the destroy route has its own <code>errorElement</code> and is a child of the root route, the error will render there instead of the root. As you probably noticed, these errors bubble up to the nearest <code>errorElement</code>. Add as many or as few as you like, as long as you've got one at the root.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-index-routes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#index-routes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Index Routes</h2>
<p dir="auto">When we load up the app, you'll notice a big blank page on the right side of our list.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/19.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/19.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">When a route has children, and you're at the parent route's path, the <code>&lt;Outlet&gt;</code> has nothing to render because no children match. You can think of index routes as the default child route to fill in that space.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the index route module</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="touch src/routes/index.jsx"><pre class="notranslate"><code>touch src/routes/index.jsx
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Fill in the index component's elements</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Feel free to copy paste, nothing special here.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export default function Index() {
  return (
    &lt;p id=&quot;zero-state&quot;&gt;
      This is a demo for React Router.
      &lt;br /&gt;
      Check out{&quot; &quot;}
      &lt;a href=&quot;https://reactrouter.com/&quot;&gt;
        the docs at reactrouter.com
      &lt;/a&gt;
      .
    &lt;/p&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Index</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"zero-state"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      This is a demo for React Router.
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">br</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      Check out<span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">" "</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">href</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"https://reactrouter.com/"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        the docs at reactrouter.com
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">a</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      .
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Configure the index route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code
import Index from &quot;./routes/index&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    action: rootAction,
    children: [
      { index: true, element: &lt;Index /&gt; },
      /* existing routes */
    ],
  },
]);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Index</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"./routes/index"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">loader</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">index</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Index</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c">/* existing routes */</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note the <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/route#index"><code>{ index:true }</code></a> instead of <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/route#path"><code>{ path: "" }</code></a>. That tells the router to match and render this route when the user is at the parent route's exact path, so there are no other child routes to render in the <code>&lt;Outlet&gt;</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/20.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/20.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Voila! No more blank space. It's common to put dashboards, stats, feeds, etc. at index routes. They can participate in data loading as well.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-cancel-button" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#cancel-button"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Cancel Button</h2>
<p dir="auto">On the edit page we've got a cancel button that doesn't do anything yet. We'd like it to do the same thing as the browser's back button.</p>
<p dir="auto">We'll need a click handler on the button as well as <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-navigate"><code>useNavigate</code></a> from React Router.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the cancel button click handler with <code>useNavigate</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  Form,
  useLoaderData,
  redirect,
  useNavigate,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function Edit() {
  const contact = useLoaderData();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  return (
    &lt;Form method=&quot;post&quot; id=&quot;contact-form&quot;&gt;
      {/* existing code */}

      &lt;p&gt;
        &lt;button type=&quot;submit&quot;&gt;Save&lt;/button&gt;
        &lt;button
          type=&quot;button&quot;
          onClick={() =&gt; {
            navigate(-1);
          }}
        &gt;
          Cancel
        &lt;/button&gt;
      &lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;/Form&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">redirect</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useNavigate</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Edit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">navigate</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useNavigate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">method</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"post"</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"contact-form"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>

      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span> <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"submit"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>Save<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"button"</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">onClick</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">navigate</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          Cancel
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Now when the user clicks "Cancel", they'll be sent back one entry in the browser's history.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="monocle_face" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f9d0.png">🧐</g-emoji> Why is there no <code>event.preventDefault</code> on the button?</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">A <code>&lt;button type="button"&gt;</code>, while seemingly redundant, is the HTML way of preventing a button from submitting its form.</p>
<p dir="auto">Two more features to go. We're on the home stretch!</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-url-search-params-and-get-submissions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#url-search-params-and-get-submissions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>URL Search Params and GET Submissions</h2>
<p dir="auto">All of our interactive UI so far have been either links that change the URL or forms that post data to actions. The search field is interesting because it's a mix of both: it's a form but it only changes the URL, it doesn't change data.</p>
<p dir="auto">Right now it's just a normal HTML <code>&lt;form&gt;</code>, not a React Router <code>&lt;Form&gt;</code>. Let's see what the browser does with it by default:</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Type a name into the search field and hit the enter key</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Note the browser's URL now contains your query in the URL as <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/URLSearchParams" rel="nofollow">URLSearchParams</a>:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="http://127.0.0.1:5173/?q=ryan"><pre class="notranslate"><code>http://127.0.0.1:5173/?q=ryan
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If we review the search form, it looks like this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
  &lt;input
    id=&quot;q&quot;
    aria-label=&quot;Search contacts&quot;
    placeholder=&quot;Search&quot;
    type=&quot;search&quot;
    name=&quot;q&quot;
  /&gt;
  &lt;div id=&quot;search-spinner&quot; aria-hidden hidden={true} /&gt;
  &lt;div className=&quot;sr-only&quot; aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/form&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">form</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-form"</span> <span class="pl-c1">role</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">aria-label</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Search contacts"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">placeholder</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Search"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-spinner"</span> <span class="pl-c1">aria-hidden</span> <span class="pl-c1">hidden</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">className</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sr-only"</span> <span class="pl-c1">aria-live</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"polite"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">As we've seen before, browsers can serialize forms by the <code>name</code> attribute of it's input elements. The name of this input is <code>q</code>, that's why the URL has <code>?q=</code>. If we named it <code>search</code> the URL would be <code>?search=</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that this form is different from the others we've used, it does not have <code>&lt;form method="post"&gt;</code>. The default <code>method</code> is <code>"get"</code>. That means when the browser creates the request for the next document, it doesn't put the form data into the request POST body, but into the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/URLSearchParams" rel="nofollow"><code>URLSearchParams</code></a> of a GET request.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-get-submissions-with-client-side-routing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-submissions-with-client-side-routing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>GET Submissions with Client Side Routing</h2>
<p dir="auto">Let's use client side routing to submit this form and filter the list in our existing loader.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Change <code>&lt;form&gt;</code> to <code>&lt;Form&gt;</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;Form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
  &lt;input
    id=&quot;q&quot;
    aria-label=&quot;Search contacts&quot;
    placeholder=&quot;Search&quot;
    type=&quot;search&quot;
    name=&quot;q&quot;
  /&gt;
  &lt;div id=&quot;search-spinner&quot; aria-hidden hidden={true} /&gt;
  &lt;div className=&quot;sr-only&quot; aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/Form&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-form"</span> <span class="pl-c1">role</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">aria-label</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Search contacts"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">placeholder</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"Search"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search"</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-spinner"</span> <span class="pl-c1">aria-hidden</span> <span class="pl-c1">hidden</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">className</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sr-only"</span> <span class="pl-c1">aria-live</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"polite"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Filter the list if there are URLSearchParams</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export async function loader({ request }) {
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  const q = url.searchParams.get(&quot;q&quot;);
  const contacts = await getContacts(q);
  return { contacts };
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">loader</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> request <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">url</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">url</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">q</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">url</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">searchParams</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contacts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">getContacts</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">q</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/21.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/21.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Because this is a GET, not a POST, React Router <em>does not</em> call the <code>action</code>. Submitting a GET form is the same as clicking a link: only the URL changes. That's why the code we added for filtering is in the <code>loader</code>, not the <code>action</code> of this route.</p>
<p dir="auto">This also means it's a normal page navigation. You can click the back button to get back to where you were.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-synchronizing-urls-to-form-state" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#synchronizing-urls-to-form-state"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Synchronizing URLs to Form State</h2>
<p dir="auto">There are a couple of UX issues here that we can take care of quickly.</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>If you click back after a search, the form field still has the value you entered even though the list is no longer filtered.</li>
<li>If you refresh the page after searching, the form field no longer has the value in it, even though the list is filtered</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">In other words, the URL and our form state are out of sync.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Return <code>q</code> from your loader and set it as the search field default value</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code

export async function loader({ request }) {
  const url = new URL(request.url);
  const q = url.searchParams.get(&quot;q&quot;);
  const contacts = await getContacts(q);
  return { contacts, q };
}

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts, q } = useLoaderData();
  const navigation = useNavigation();

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;React Router Contacts&lt;/h1&gt;
        &lt;div&gt;
          &lt;Form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
            &lt;input
              id=&quot;q&quot;
              aria-label=&quot;Search contacts&quot;
              placeholder=&quot;Search&quot;
              type=&quot;search&quot;
              name=&quot;q&quot;
              defaultValue={q}
            /&gt;
            {/* existing code */}
          &lt;/Form&gt;
          {/* existing code */}
        &lt;/div&gt;
        {/* existing code */}
      &lt;/div&gt;
      {/* existing code */}
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">url</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-c1">URL</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">url</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">q</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">url</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">searchParams</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contacts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">getContacts</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">q</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts<span class="pl-kos">,</span> q <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts<span class="pl-kos">,</span> q <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">navigation</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useNavigation</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>React Router Contacts<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
