<p dir="auto">That solves problem (2). If you refresh the page now, the input field will show the query.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/21.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/21.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now for problem (1), clicking the back button and updating the input. We can bring in <code>useEffect</code> from React to manipulate the form's state in the DOM directly.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Synchronize input value with the URL Search Params</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { useEffect } from &quot;react&quot;;

// existing code

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts, q } = useLoaderData();
  const navigation = useNavigation();

  useEffect(() =&gt; {
    document.getElementById(&quot;q&quot;).value = q;
  }, [q]);

  // existing code
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">useEffect</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts<span class="pl-kos">,</span> q <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">navigation</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useNavigation</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-en">useEffect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getElementById</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">q</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">[</span><span class="pl-s1">q</span><span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="thinking" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f914.png">🤔</g-emoji> Shouldn't you use a controlled component and React State for this?</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">You could certainly do this as a controlled component, but you'll end up with more complexity for the same behavior. You don't control the URL, the user does with the back/forward buttons. There would be more synchronization points with a controlled component.</p>
<details>
<summary>If you're still concerned, expand this to see what it would look like</summary>
<p dir="auto">Notice how controlling the input requires three points of synchronization now instead of just one. The behavior is identical but the code is more complex.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import { useEffect, useState } from &quot;react&quot;;
// existing code

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts, q } = useLoaderData();
  const [query, setQuery] = useState(q);
  const navigation = useNavigation();

  useEffect(() =&gt; {
    setQuery(q);
  }, [q]);

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;React Router Contacts&lt;/h1&gt;
        &lt;div&gt;
          &lt;Form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
            &lt;input
              id=&quot;q&quot;
              aria-label=&quot;Search contacts&quot;
              placeholder=&quot;Search&quot;
              type=&quot;search&quot;
              name=&quot;q&quot;
              value={query}
              onChange={(e) =&gt; {

          {/* existing code */}
        &lt;/div&gt;
        {/* existing code */}

</details>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-submitting-forms-onchange" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#submitting-forms-onchange"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Submitting Forms <code>onChange</code></h2>
<p dir="auto">We've got a product decision to make here. For this UI, we'd probably rather have the filtering happen on every key stroke instead of when the form is explicitly submitted.</p>
<p dir="auto">We've seen <code>useNavigate</code> already, we'll use its cousin, <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-submit"><code>useSubmit</code></a>, for this.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code
import {
  // existing code
  useSubmit,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts, q } = useLoaderData();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const submit = useSubmit();

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;React Router Contacts&lt;/h1&gt;
        &lt;div&gt;
          &lt;Form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
            &lt;input
              id=&quot;q&quot;
              aria-label=&quot;Search contacts&quot;
              placeholder=&quot;Search&quot;
              type=&quot;search&quot;
              name=&quot;q&quot;
              defaultValue={q}
              onChange={(event) =&gt; {
                submit(event.currentTarget.form);
              }}
            /&gt;
            {/* existing code */}
          &lt;/Form&gt;
          {/* existing code */}
        &lt;/div&gt;
        {/* existing code */}

      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Now as you type, the form is submitted automatically!</p>
<p dir="auto">Note the argument to <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-submit"><code>submit</code></a>. We're passing in <code>event.currentTarget.form</code>. The <code>currentTarget</code> is the DOM node the event is attached to, and the <code>currentTarget.form</code> is the input's parent form node. The <code>submit</code> function will serialize and submit any form you pass to it.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-adding-search-spinner" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#adding-search-spinner"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Adding Search Spinner</h2>
<p dir="auto">In a production app, it's likely this search will be looking for records in a database that is too large to send all at once and filter client side. That's why this demo has some faked network latency.</p>
<p dir="auto">Without any loading indicator, the search feels kinda sluggish. Even if we could make our database faster, we'll always have the user's network latency in the way and out of our control. For a better UX, let's add some immediate UI feedback for the search. For this we'll use <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-navigation"><code>useNavigation</code></a> again.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Add the search spinner</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code

export default function Root() {
  const { contacts, q } = useLoaderData();
  const navigation = useNavigation();
  const submit = useSubmit();

  const searching =
    navigation.location &amp;&amp;
    new URLSearchParams(navigation.location.search).has(
      &quot;q&quot;
    );

  useEffect(() =&gt; {
    document.getElementById(&quot;q&quot;).value = q;
  }, [q]);

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;React Router Contacts&lt;/h1&gt;
        &lt;div&gt;
          &lt;Form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
            &lt;input
              id=&quot;q&quot;
              className={searching ? &quot;loading&quot; : &quot;&quot;}
              // existing code
            /&gt;
            &lt;div
              id=&quot;search-spinner&quot;
              aria-hidden
              hidden={!searching}
            /&gt;
            {/* existing code */}
          &lt;/Form&gt;
          {/* existing code */}
        &lt;/div&gt;
        {/* existing code */}
      &lt;/div&gt;
      {/* existing code */}
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> contacts<span class="pl-kos">,</span> q <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">navigation</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useNavigation</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">submit</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useSubmit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">searching</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">navigation</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">location</span> <span class="pl-c1">&amp;&amp;</span>
    <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">URLSearchParams</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">navigation</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">location</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">search</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">has</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
      <span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-en">useEffect</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-smi">document</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">getElementById</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">q</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>React Router Contacts<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-form"</span> <span class="pl-c1">role</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">className</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">searching</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"loading"</span> : <span class="pl-s">""</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
              <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-spinner"</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">aria-hidden</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">hidden</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">searching</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/22.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/22.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">The <code>navigation.location</code> will show up when the app is navigating to a new URL and loading the data for it. It then goes away when there is no pending navigation anymore.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-managing-the-history-stack" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#managing-the-history-stack"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Managing the History Stack</h2>
<p dir="auto">Now that the form is submitted for every key stroke, if we type the characters "seba" and then delete them with backspace, we end up with 7 new entries in the stack <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="joy" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f602.png">😂</g-emoji>. We definitely don't want this</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/23.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/23.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We can avoid this by <em>replacing</em> the current entry in the history stack with the next page, instead of pushing into it.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Use <code>replace</code> in <code>submit</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code

export default function Root() {
  // existing code

  return (
    &lt;&gt;
      &lt;div id=&quot;sidebar&quot;&gt;
        &lt;h1&gt;React Router Contacts&lt;/h1&gt;
        &lt;div&gt;
          &lt;Form id=&quot;search-form&quot; role=&quot;search&quot;&gt;
            &lt;input
              id=&quot;q&quot;
              // existing code
              onChange={(event) =&gt; {
                const isFirstSearch = q == null;
                submit(event.currentTarget.form, {
                  replace: !isFirstSearch,
                });
              }}
            /&gt;
            {/* existing code */}
          &lt;/Form&gt;
          {/* existing code */}
        &lt;/div&gt;
        {/* existing code */}
      &lt;/div&gt;
      {/* existing code */}
    &lt;/&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Root</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"sidebar"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>React Router Contacts<span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">h1</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search-form"</span> <span class="pl-c1">role</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"search"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">input</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">id</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"q"</span>
              <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
              <span class="pl-c1">onChange</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">event</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
                <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">isFirstSearch</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">q</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
                <span class="pl-en">submit</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">event</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">currentTarget</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
                  <span class="pl-c1">replace</span>: <span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">isFirstSearch</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
                <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
              <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
            <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">div</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">We only want to replace search results, not the page before we started searching, so we do a quick check if this is the first search or not and then decide to replace.</p>
<p dir="auto">Each key stroke no longer creates new entries, so the user can click back out of the search results without having to click it 7 times <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="sweat_smile" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f605.png">😅</g-emoji>.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-mutations-without-navigation" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mutations-without-navigation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Mutations Without Navigation</h2>
<p dir="auto">So far all of our mutations (the times we change data) have used forms that navigate, creating new entries in the history stack. While these user flows are common, it's equally as common to want to change data <em>without</em> causing a navigation.</p>
<p dir="auto">For these cases, we have the <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-fetcher"><code>useFetcher</code></a> hook. It allows us to communicate with loaders and actions without causing a navigation.</p>
<p dir="auto">The ★ button on the contact page makes sense for this. We aren't creating or deleting a new record, we don't want to change pages, we simply want to change the data on the page we're looking at.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Change the <code>&lt;Favorite&gt;</code> form to a fetcher form</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  useLoaderData,
  Form,
  useFetcher,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

// existing code

function Favorite({ contact }) {
  const fetcher = useFetcher();
  let favorite = contact.favorite;

  return (
    &lt;fetcher.Form method=&quot;post&quot;&gt;
      &lt;button
        name=&quot;favorite&quot;
        value={favorite ? &quot;false&quot; : &quot;true&quot;}
        aria-label={
          favorite
            ? &quot;Remove from favorites&quot;
            : &quot;Add to favorites&quot;
        }
      &gt;
        {favorite ? &quot;★&quot; : &quot;☆&quot;}
      &lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;/fetcher.Form&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useLoaderData</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">useFetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Favorite</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> contact <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useFetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">favorite</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">method</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"post"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"favorite"</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">value</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"false"</span> : <span class="pl-s">"true"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">aria-label</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">favorite</span>
            ? <span class="pl-s">"Remove from favorites"</span>
            : <span class="pl-s">"Add to favorites"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"★"</span> : <span class="pl-s">"☆"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Might want to take a look at that form while we're here. As always, our form has fields with a <code>name</code> prop. This form will send <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/FormData" rel="nofollow"><code>formData</code></a> with a <code>favorite</code> key that's either <code>"true" | "false"</code>. Since it's got <code>method="post"</code> it will call the action. Since there is no <code>&lt;fetcher.Form action="..."&gt;</code> prop, it will post to the route where the form is rendered.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Create the action</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code
import { getContact, updateContact } from &quot;../contacts&quot;;

export async function action({ request, params }) {
  let formData = await request.formData();
  return updateContact(params.contactId, {
    favorite: formData.get(&quot;favorite&quot;) === &quot;true&quot;,
  });
}

export default function Contact() {
  // existing code
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-s1">getContact</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">updateContact</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"../contacts"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">action</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> request<span class="pl-kos">,</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">formData</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-s1">request</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">updateContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">favorite</span>: <span class="pl-s1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"favorite"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"true"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">default</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Contact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Pretty simple. Pull the form data off the request and send it to the data model.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Configure the route's new action</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code
import Contact, {
  loader as contactLoader,
  action as contactAction,
} from &quot;./routes/contact&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    action: rootAction,
    children: [
      { index: true, element: &lt;Index /&gt; },
      {
        path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
        element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
        loader: contactLoader,
        action: contactAction,
      },
      /* existing code */
    ],
  },
]);"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Contact</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">loader</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">contactLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">action</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">contactAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">loader</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">index</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Index</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c">/* existing code */</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alright, we're ready to click the star next to the user's name!</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/24.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/24.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Check that out, both stars automatically update. Our new <code>&lt;fetcher.Form method="post"&gt;</code> works almost exactly like a the <code>&lt;Form&gt;</code> we've been using: it calls the action and then all data is revalidated automatically--even your errors will be caught the same way.</p>
<p dir="auto">There is one key difference though, it's not a navigation--the URL doesn't change, the history stack is unaffected.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-optimistic-ui" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#optimistic-ui"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Optimistic UI</h2>
<p dir="auto">You probably noticed the app felt kind of unresponsive when we clicked the the favorite button from the last section. Once again, we added some network latency because you're going to have it in the real world!</p>
<p dir="auto">To give the user some feedback, we could put the star into a loading state with <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/hooks/use-fetcher#fetcherstate"><code>fetcher.state</code></a> (a lot like <code>navigation.state</code> from before), but we can do something even better this time. We can use a strategy called "optimistic UI"</p>
<p dir="auto">The fetcher knows the form data being submitted to the action, so it's available to you on <code>fetcher.formData</code>. We'll use that to immediately update the star's state, even though the network hasn't finished. If the update eventually fails, the UI will revert to the real data.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Read the optimistic value from <code>fetcher.formData</code></strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// existing code

function Favorite({ contact }) {
  const fetcher = useFetcher();

  let favorite = contact.favorite;
  if (fetcher.formData) {
    favorite = fetcher.formData.get(&quot;favorite&quot;) === &quot;true&quot;;
  }

  return (
    &lt;fetcher.Form method=&quot;post&quot;&gt;
      &lt;button
        name=&quot;favorite&quot;
        value={favorite ? &quot;false&quot; : &quot;true&quot;}
        aria-label={
          favorite
            ? &quot;Remove from favorites&quot;
            : &quot;Add to favorites&quot;
        }
      &gt;
        {favorite ? &quot;★&quot; : &quot;☆&quot;}
      &lt;/button&gt;
    &lt;/fetcher.Form&gt;
  );
}"><pre><span class="pl-c">// existing code</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-v">Favorite</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> contact <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">useFetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">favorite</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">formData</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">get</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">"favorite"</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">===</span> <span class="pl-s">"true"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">Form</span> <span class="pl-c1">method</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"post"</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"favorite"</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">value</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"false"</span> : <span class="pl-s">"true"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">aria-label</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
          <span class="pl-s1">favorite</span>
            ? <span class="pl-s">"Remove from favorites"</span>
            : <span class="pl-s">"Add to favorites"</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">favorite</span> ? <span class="pl-s">"★"</span> : <span class="pl-s">"☆"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">button</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-s1">fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-v">Form</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If you click the button now you should see the star <em>immediately</em> change to the new state. Instead of always rendering the actual data, we check if the fetcher has any <code>formData</code> being submitted, if so, we'll use that instead. When the action is done, the <code>fetcher.formData</code> will no longer exist and we're back to using the actual data. So even if you write bugs in your optimistic UI code, it'll eventually go back to the correct state 🥹</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-not-found-data" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#not-found-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Not Found Data</h2>
<p dir="auto">What happens if the contact we're trying to load doesn't exist?</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/25.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/25.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Our root <a href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/docs/route/error-element"><code>errorElement</code></a> is catching this unexpected error as we try to render a <code>null</code> contact. Nice the error was properly handled, but we can do better!</p>
<p dir="auto">Whenever you have an expected error case in a loader or action–like the data not existing–you can <code>throw</code>. The call stack will break, React Router will catch it, and the error path is rendered instead. We won't even try to render a <code>null</code> contact.</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Throw a 404 response in the loader</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export async function loader({ params }) {
  const contact = await getContact(params.contactId);
  if (!contact) {
    throw new Response(&quot;&quot;, {
      status: 404,
      statusText: &quot;Not Found&quot;,
    });
  }
  return contact;
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">export</span> <span class="pl-k">async</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">loader</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span> params <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-k">await</span> <span class="pl-en">getContact</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">params</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">contactId</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-c1">!</span><span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-k">throw</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-v">Response</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">""</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">status</span>: <span class="pl-c1">404</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">statusText</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Not Found"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">contact</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/27.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/27.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Instead of hitting a render error with <code>Cannot read properties of null</code>, we avoid the component completely and render the error path instead, telling the user something more specific.</p>
<p dir="auto">This keeps your happy paths, happy. Your route elements don't need to concern themselves with error and loading states.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-pathless-routes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pathless-routes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Pathless Routes</h2>
<p dir="auto">One last thing. The last error page we saw would be better if it rendered inside the root outlet, instead of the whole page. In fact, every error in all of our child routes would be better in the outlet, then the user has more options than hitting refresh.</p>
<p dir="auto">We'd like it to look like this:</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/remix-run/react-router/blob/main/_docs/tutorial/26.webp"><img src="/remix-run/react-router/raw/main/_docs/tutorial/26.webp" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">We could add the error element to every one of the child routes but, since it's all the same error page, this isn't recommended.</p>
<p dir="auto">There's a cleaner way. Routes can be used <em>without</em> a path, which lets them participate in the UI layout without requiring new path segments in the URL. Check it out:</p>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="point_right" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f449.png">👉</g-emoji> <strong>Wrap the child routes in a pathless route</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="createBrowserRouter([
  {
    path: &quot;/&quot;,
    element: &lt;Root /&gt;,
    loader: rootLoader,
    action: rootAction,
    errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
    children: [
      {
        errorElement: &lt;ErrorPage /&gt;,
        children: [
          { index: true, element: &lt;Index /&gt; },
          {
            path: &quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;,
            element: &lt;Contact /&gt;,
            loader: contactLoader,
            action: contactAction,
          },
          /* the rest of the routes */
        ],
      },
    ],
  },
]);"><pre><span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">[</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"/"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">loader</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">rootAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">children</span>: <span class="pl-kos">[</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span> <span class="pl-c1">index</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Index</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">path</span>: <span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">element</span>: <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">loader</span>: <span class="pl-s1">contactLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
            <span class="pl-c1">action</span>: <span class="pl-s1">contactAction</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
          <span class="pl-c">/* the rest of the routes */</span>
        <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
      <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">]</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">When any errors are thrown in the child routes, our new pathless route will catch it and render, preserving the root route's UI!</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-jsx-routes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#jsx-routes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>JSX Routes</h2>
<p dir="auto">And for our final trick, many folks prefer to configure their routes with JSX. You can do that with <code>createRoutesFromElements</code>. There is no functional difference between JSX or objects when configuring your routes, it's simply a stylistic preference.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import {
  createRoutesFromElements,
  createBrowserRouter,
} from &quot;react-router-dom&quot;;

const router = createBrowserRouter(
  createRoutesFromElements(
    &lt;Route
      path=&quot;/&quot;
      element={&lt;Root /&gt;}
      loader={rootLoader}
      action={rootAction}
      errorElement={&lt;ErrorPage /&gt;}
    &gt;
      &lt;Route errorElement={&lt;ErrorPage /&gt;}&gt;
        &lt;Route index element={&lt;Index /&gt;} /&gt;
        &lt;Route
          path=&quot;contacts/:contactId&quot;
          element={&lt;Contact /&gt;}
          loader={contactLoader}
          action={contactAction}
        /&gt;
        &lt;Route
          path=&quot;contacts/:contactId/edit&quot;
          element={&lt;EditContact /&gt;}
          loader={contactLoader}
          action={editAction}
        /&gt;
        &lt;Route
          path=&quot;contacts/:contactId/destroy&quot;
          action={destroyAction}
        /&gt;
      &lt;/Route&gt;
    &lt;/Route&gt;
  )
);"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">createRoutesFromElements</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s">"react-router-dom"</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">router</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">createBrowserRouter</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
  <span class="pl-en">createRoutesFromElements</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">path</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"/"</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">element</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Root</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">loader</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">rootLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">rootAction</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span> <span class="pl-c1">errorElement</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">ErrorPage</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span> <span class="pl-c1">index</span> <span class="pl-c1">element</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Index</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">path</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId"</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">element</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Contact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">loader</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contactLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contactAction</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">path</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId/edit"</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">element</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">EditContact</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">loader</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">contactLoader</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">editAction</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">path</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"contacts/:contactId/destroy"</span>
          <span class="pl-c1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">destroyAction</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
      <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-ent">Route</span><span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">)</span>
<span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<p dir="auto">That's it! Thanks for giving React Router a shot. We hope this tutorial gives you a solid start to build great user experiences. There's a lot more you can do with React Router, so make sure to check out all the APIs <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="grinning" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f600.png">😀</g-emoji></p>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>

  </readme-toc>
